<rate>3<//rate>< Review>
Average coffee, average pastries. Main perk is the late operating hours and plentiful seating. Also the bus stop right outside allows some piece of mind for those taking the bus home late. The establishment itself is fairly run-down feeling and the restroom doesn't radiate a sense of hygiene. Some of the outlets are very loose so woe to anyone who has a Mac or other heavy charger because it will not stay in. Select your table and chairs carefully, lots of wobblyness!</Review>

< Text>
Just strolled in here through an open door. The woman behind the counter said something I couldn't hear over the construction noise. I came around to the counter so we wouldn't have to speak across the sneeze guard and she angrily threw her arms out repeatedly, shooing me away with a scowl on her face. She caught herself and put on a strained and facetious smile to say they were closed, but it was too late for me. Everyone is tired in the morning, especially people looking for coffee. Being straight up rude isn't a way to treat your customers. If you're closed, close your door, or put your shoddily handwritten sign somewhere it can be seen. Don't punish people for wanting to buy things from you. I work in the neighborhood but hadn't visited this place until today. Needless to say, I won't be coming back.<//Text>

<text>My cappuccino review: poor. I ordered a double capp and what I got was an explosion of foam. Seriously over half of the cup was foam, and it was more like styrofoam than what I would like to see of coffee. The person who made this cup of coffee steamed the milk into oblivion where all that was left was super stiff tasteless foam and slightly overcooked milk. Topping that off was the harshness of the coffee, it was either made from low cost beans or they just don't know how to pull a good espresso from their machine. Peet's provides a much better capp than this place.

I won't be trying their capp again or any espresso drinks, once burned is enough for me, though I will go back and try their normal coffee at some point.

Ambiance: good. A fair number of tables with wifi and power, it's nice enough that it earns a star just for the feel of support for folks who want to get something done. <text>What a pleasant and festive way to spend Christmas Eve, especially during the craziness of 2020 !  The Harbor Lights Cruise is a perfect relaxing way to ring in the Holiday Season.
The staff and crew are a relaxed but professional group that made getting tickets, checking in and boarding very easy, while upholding safety standards.  The boat was disinfected and cleaned between nightly cruises.  I'm certain I will be back to take the cruise in December 2021.  If you haven't been before, you have to try it.

<pics>None< /pics>< text>
we had a great time with our family of 8. it was our first time doing a harbor cruise. valet was full but friendly and willing to accommodate us.  a bit of confusion during booking  as the website link i clicked said cruises 5:30 , 7, or 8:30 but redirected to a general ticketing page with more options available. ultimately it was my error booking on a cell phone and not checking my confirmation email; led to us missing the 4:30 cruise that i booked by mistake instead of the 5:30. by that time the 5:30 cruise was completely booked and we were put on a wait list. knowing its hard to accommodate our large family anyways, we walked down the boardwalk to find dinner and check out the fun zone.

5 stars earned: the hero of the company left his station at the (very busy) check in area to find our group in a little pizza place down the boardwalk, recognized me, and hand delivered our boarding passes for 5:30. "squeezing us into a fully booked charter", we were expecting a very crowded boat but were happy to find that on this fully booked boat there was plenty of room to walk around, and booths available inside by the fully stocked bar.

70 min cruise is the perfect amount of time with our 4 young children, (2 restless toddlers)  as we were able to see everything in that time.  we spent most of the cruise standing and walking around the boat (easily i might add) this leads me to believe alot of the bad reviews here have been addressed and this is a company that really listens to and cares about their customers.

we plan to do it again next year and also plan to do a deep sea fishing charter this summer.</text>

< review>
We went on the last Christmas Boat parade tour which left at 8:30PM on Sunday.  It was a little confusing on which line to stand in since there was a 8:10pm tour and our tour.  Turns out we were in the 8:10 line but when we got to the end of the line we found ourselves at the beginning of the 8:30 line...so not a problem.

The captain did an excellent job of pointing out interesting homes and boats to focus on.  He also got us out to his favorite spot for both some beautiful homes and a few businesses.  Great tour...well worth it and very enjoyable.  Will do again...good value.  And no rain even though it was predicted.</review>

<rating>5</rating><Review>Excellent Thai restaurant. Waitress was prompt, polite, and professional. Food arrived quickly, was of high quality, and was perfectly seasoned. Prices are fair and portions are generous. I ordered the Thai Basil (Pad Graw Prow), chicken, Thai hot. The chicken pieces were juicy and on the larger size, which I prefer, and the chili sauce was sweet with enough of a syrupy character to nicely coat the vegetables and chicken. There were plenty of chopped Bird peppers to get the heat level up, although this dish today was not what I'd consider a "10" on the heat scale, more like 8.5. I feel confident that they could make it hotter if requested.

This is a young restaurant, and it warmed my heart to see lots of people coming in to eat as we were eating. I want to eat here again on my next visit to Fort Bragg!< /Review>< Pics>

I was the first customer of the day as was greeted by the owner and again at the counter by a cashier. 1620520003908</Date>
< Rating>
3</Rating>
< Text>
I love Indian food and have tried several restaurants throughout the so Cal area. I was excited to try Flavor of India. However I was left feeling unsatisfied with the entire experience.

After waiting for a table on a busy Friday night, I was finally seated only to wait another additional 20 minutes before anybody came to take my order. I ordered samosas,  chicken Tikka, lamb vindaloo,  Naan,  and rice.
The samosas were not that great. It was rather dull in taste and complexity compared to the fragrance of spices I'm accustomed to in Samosas.
After waiting for another 20 mins, the food starting to come one by one. First was the chicken Tikka. Again. Disappointing from the chicken Tikka I have had other places. Not to say it was bad, but it lacked the unique char and smoked taste that is the signature taste of anything made in the clay oven. It just tasted like regular ol chicken fajitas.
Next the lamb vindaloo. Again the trend continues. Something lacking in the overall flavor profile compared to other versions I've tried.
The saag alo was good, however the potatoes were UNDERCOOKED and just ruined the dish for me. The rice that I ordered never came. Which was just disappointing. Nobody ever came to check on me for well over 30 mins. By the time I could get somebody, to tell them about the rice. The kitchen was already closed. It was just a disappointing experience for me overall and won't be back. The food is by no means bad, it's just not that great either. I think there are much better places to get your Indian fix on.</Text>

< review>
Flavor of India is conveniently located in Downtown Burbank. I've never been a fan of Indian food, but since it's been years since I last tried it, I decided to give it a go.

Surprise! Palate was very happy this go around. The garlic naan was incredible. Tandoori chicken was a bit dry, but the sauce was very well done. The butter chicken & tikka masala didn't taste very different to me, but they were both good. The real difference that I could tell was the texture of the sauces. Finally, we also got the vegetable korma, which was my favorite. The food was flavorful and at a good price range, and the service was good. Do keep in mind that I have nothing to compare this experience to, but rather I rate this as an Indian food first timer.

Thank you Flavor of India for awakening my taste buds for Indian food. I'm now aware of a whole cuisine that I have been missing out on.  Great LA local business.</review>
